# New Category : Pizza Boxes

## **Hero Section**

**Pizza Boxes**

Hot, sturdy, and ready to deliver. Buy pizza boxes wholesale for restaurants, takeout chains, and food delivery brands that value quality, freshness, and presentation.

## **Overview**

**Custom Pizza Boxes**

Our pizza packaging boxes combine heat resistance, strength, and branding value. Whether you serve thin crust, deep dish, or cheesy slices, these boxes keep your pizza warm and intact until the first bite. Each design enhances your brand appeal while protecting freshness and flavor.

At BoxyPack, we create custom pizza boxes that match your restaurant’s image and service style. From small snack boxes to extra-large family packs, we customize every box with your logo, colors, and message.

## **Key Features**

* Ventilation holes to prevent sogginess

* Custom logo and print design options

* Available in all standard and custom sizes

* Foldable and stackable for easy storage

* 100% recyclable and eco-friendly materials

* Perfect for dine-in, delivery, and takeout restaurants

**What Are Pizza Boxes?**

Pizza boxes are food packaging containers designed to carry, protect, and preserve the temperature of pizzas during transport. They prevent heat loss, resist oil absorption, and maintain crispness, ensuring your customers enjoy the same quality at home as in your restaurant.

These boxes come in standard square, rectangular, and custom shapes, suitable for different pizza sizes and branding goals. Each one is strong enough to hold hot pizzas securely without bending or leaking.

## **Which Material Is Used in Pizza Boxes?**

Our pizza boxes are made from food-grade corrugated and kraft paperboard to ensure hygiene, safety, and durability. The material keeps pizzas warm, prevents grease penetration, and supports custom printing for brand recognition.

We also offer:

* **Corrugated Board** for temperature retention and strength

* **Kraft Paperboard** for eco-friendly pizza packaging

* **White Cardboard** for premium printing and clean look

* **Grease-Resistant Coatings** for oil control

* **Ventilated Designs** for moisture release and crisp texture

Each material is carefully selected to deliver freshness, protection, and sustainability in every order.

## **Our Range of Pizza Boxes**

We supply pizza packaging wholesale for all types of businesses  from small local shops to large pizza chains. Our collection includes single-slice boxes, family-size cartons, and printed promotional packaging. Whether you want a simple kraft look or colorful branding, BoxyPack ensures your boxes make every delivery look professional and appetizing.

## **Why Choose Our Pizza Boxes**

At BoxyPack, function meets flavor. Our custom pizza boxes are built to protect your food while boosting your brand image.

**Food-Safe Design:** Certified, hygienic, and odor-free packaging.  
**Eco-Friendly Build:** Made from recyclable paper materials.  
**Full Customization:** Add logo, color, and taglines that reflect your brand.

## **What Are Cosmetic Boxes?**

Cosmetic boxes are packaging solutions created to protect and present beauty products attractively. They prevent damage, leakage, and exposure to light or moisture, ensuring product integrity and shelf appeal.

These boxes also carry your brand story, making every product feel exclusive and trustworthy. Available in folding cartons, magnetic rigid boxes, and window display styles, they add both beauty and durability to your product line.

## **Which Material Is Used in Cosmetic Boxes?**

Our cosmetic boxes are made from premium paperboard, rigid board, and kraft materials. Each option combines structure with elegance, offering high-quality printing and texture that matches your brand’s tone.

We also offer:

* **White Cardboard** for clean, sharp printing results

* **Rigid Chipboard** for luxury cosmetic boxes

* **Kraft Paperboard** for eco-conscious packaging

## **What Are Chocolate Boxes?**

Chocolate boxes are packaging containers designed to store and display chocolates in a safe, elegant, and temperature-conscious way. They protect delicate treats from external factors like heat, moisture, and handling while presenting them in a refined, gift-ready design.

These boxes boost brand identity while ensuring customers enjoy a clean and satisfying dining experience at home or on the go.

Each material is selected to ensure safety, performance, and eco-friendly packaging solutions.

### **Product Overview**

Our kraft candle boxes are crafted from high-quality recycled kraft paperboard, offering a strong, rustic, and environmentally friendly packaging solution. These boxes protect candles from breakage, dust, and heat exposure while giving your brand an organic, handmade appeal. Ideal for natural candle brands, eco-conscious makers, gift boutiques, wellness stores, and artisanal collections, these boxes blend durability with sustainability.

At BoxyPack, we create custom kraft candle packaging boxes tailored to your jar size, fragrance line, and branding style. Choose from tuck-end boxes, window boxes, two-piece kraft sets, rigid kraft boxes, or kraft boxes with inserts. Each structure ensures clean folding, strong structure, and a warm, earthy look.

As a trusted custom kraft candle boxes wholesale supplier, we offer recyclable materials, precise printing, and competitive kraft candle boxes price options. Whether selling jar candles, tin candles, pillar candles, or gift-ready sets, our packaging delivers eco-friendly charm and reliable protection.
